94952SCSTG599TO	1313211796608	007439921	LEAD	TRI	2013	US COAST GUARD TRAINING CENTER PETALUMA	599 TOMALES RD	PETALUMA	SONOMA	CA	94952			YES	NO	YES	NO								611513	611519					38.257252	-122.80118									US DEPARTMENT OF HOMELAND SECURITY		Reporting Year 2013 for lead shows an increase on U.S. Coast Guard Training Center (TRACEN) Petaluma, for a combined total of 11,016 lbs.  Of that, 10,259 lbs was sent off site to four approved recycling centers and 757 lbs was sent off site as lead contaminated debris to approved RCRA Subtitled C landfills.  The reason for this particular increase is due to a large quantity reduction of uninterrupted power supply (UPS - computer and electronic device battery backup) units.  A total of 5,729 lbs came from these units that contained small sealed lead acid batteries (SSLA) to supply backup power.  The remaining 2,196 lbs from the Small Arms Firing Range and 2,334 lbs from the Motor Pool Automotive batteries were all sent off site to approved battery recycling companies.  The lower reporting of fugitive air emissions is due to two reasons.  The first one being that the TRACEN Small Arms Firing Range was shut down for maintenance and repairs from mid May 2013 until June 2014, so, there was no lead ammunition fired during this time.  The second reason is that there was an error found in the calculation of the fugitive air emissions for lead, in that Frangible Ammunition (zero lead, green ammunition) was added into the equation by mistake when it should have not been.
